style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">surmount 克服（困难/难题）= overcome</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-able 形容词后缀</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">insurmountable adj.〔困难〕难以克服的，不可逾越的</p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">insurmountable difficulties</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">难以克服的困难</strong></p><p style="white-space: 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">insurmountable</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: </strong></span></em></span>odds.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一些曾在20年前克服<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《独立日》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: </strong></em></span>task </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这几乎是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不可能的</strong>任务 </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：in the short/long run  从短期来看/从长远来看</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653544581&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=f440a410d5c9b3b5cd1823aa8eed9f68&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【in the long run】">点击链接跳转回顾【in the long run】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All our hard work will be worth it <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">in the long run</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从长远来看</strong>，我们的一切努力都是值得的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That doesn't help everyone <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">in the long run</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从长远看</strong>这没什么好处。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: run</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，问题就在这里，既然<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">短期来看</strong>…</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So what kind of jobs are you guys doing? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">When we met, what we've both been doing for most of our lives is been guiding outdoors. So, I used to be a rock climbing instructor. And then I was a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kayaking (独木舟) </strong>guide and<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> zip lining (索道滑行)</strong> guide and a glacier (冰川) guide for a little bit. And he has done lots of guiding as well. He was a glacier guide for about four years now. So he really likes guiding in the mountains and stuff, and I sort of do similar things that like not so much in the mountains a little bit more at sea level. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 16px;border-top-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-left-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Wow, that's the kind of job that people staying in <strong>office</strong> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cubicles (小格间</strong>) would envy. Because you get so much <strong>touch</strong> of the environment and nature, right? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.666" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKffRP2Q3QKhyZMCdqfytmFlgjybh1e8WDbJr2ZCpfovDpTibRxZzohzhrXxvQXxnrwOYvOic2qRricgg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="500" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">For me, I’ve been doing it for over seven years now. I've been working in that industry. And I just sort of realized after the last job that I had which ended in April this year, I don't wanna do it anymore. Because it’s sort of fun in the sense that you could be in a really cool place doing really fun activities. But as a job, it gets so boring and it's just not very challenging after a while for you, you can just be doing the same trip every single day in New Zealand. We will be doing the same trip like three times a day. Each time you have people that are doing the trip for the first time. So for them, it’s really amazing. And you have to still of keep up the interest yourself so that it still comes across as very interesting to everybody else. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I always find that after about three months of doing the same job, I can't do it anymore. So I think I want to do something more challenging in a different way. So I sort of realized that instead of doing a job that's immediately interesting like those kind of jobs, but something that's more rewarding in the long term, and stuff that we’ll are be able to like develop my skills more truly. I'm looking into different industry.</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKffRP2Q3QKhyZMCdqfytmFlV3C704ZicEBKmRfgEyuPjpcibDFosNX6ELeoAPno1iay42vowLscyGhHg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/gdGn6qialhItDoZa8g9x7M1JoN8uiazicphU2A1kBS3FdSvJfX0Upb7jzZSKaPWaazticZ5f9usiasLhyLFBibzjBw1g/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-top-left-radius: 16px;border-top-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-left-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">During your work experience, during these several years of guiding, do you have any interesting stories to share? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I definitely do. Yeah. The first one that comes to mind was, from when I was working on the glacier in New Zealand, to access the glacier, the only way is by helicopter. So we fly up in the morning and then, we would, as guides, we usually stay up on the glacier for maybe like twelve hours and they'll send up customers to me up there.  And their customers will stay for three hours each. And then I’ll fly back down. We'll get new people.</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.4125" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKffRP2Q3QKhyZMCdqfytmFlSM2st6x7icMCy26eGQKXiaxnNicKglcgjugJO23ytpwawqdz5BsdYsuCg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">But in the valley that we work where the glacier is, the weather changes really, really quickly. So if the weather changes and clouds roll into the valley, if they come in too quickly and they don't have time to send helicopters up to come and get you, you can end up having to stay on the glacier overnight because the helicopters can't come. </em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">One time I was up there, and that happened. We've flown in, I think it was seven thirty. We landed on the ice in the morning. And then, it was only about probably ten o'clock, 10 a.m. when the weather turned bad. And we were up there, it was actually a record amount of people at the time. So fifty-two customers were up there with us, and there was fifteen guides. And, you know, we have to sleep on the ice over night. So people just come up with their day pack, you know, just things that they thought they needed for the one trip. But then they end up having to sleep up there. So we have to set up tents on the ice, so we walked to safe areas of the glacier, and put up these expedition tents and have like sleeping bags and sleeping mats and a little gas stove to make food on and stuff.  So we did that and spend all night trying to chop <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">helipad (直升机停机坪)</strong> into the ice so that the helicopters can come and get us from that spot at any time. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.546875" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKffRP2Q3QKhyZMCdqfytmFl7DEqOibiblQnjde5qJIFfeLKI1cFKUMePiaJfGGRUdGNrXicLITZ43dpJw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="640" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, that was pretty crazy. One of these things were the risk is managed really well. So if you were up there on your own or if there wasn't so much in the way of preparation for those kind of circumstances, then it would probably be quite dangerous. But it’s set up in a way that no one should have any sort of issues.</em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">And everyone should be safe. And it was, it was managed well when I got stuck there  So in that sense, it was OK. It’s just very stressful because it was very cold and wet because of the clouds. And then they just stayed there the whole time. So being in the clouds was just really dump. So everything that we had was </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">drenched through (湿透了</em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</em></strong><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.stare at 凝视，盯住</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stare vt. &amp; vi. 凝视; 瞪视</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He stared at the words in complete puzzlement.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他注视著那些语句，茫然不解。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.Pleased  英/pli:zd/ 美/plizd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 高兴的；喜欢的；乐意做某事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 满意；愿意（please的过去分词形式）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was looking very pleased with himself.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他看起来飘飘然的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.dress up 穿上盛装, 打扮得漂漂亮亮</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why do they dress up as women?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们为什么要打扮成女人呢？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It didn’t matter. Lincoln also wrote in the letter to his son’s teacher, ‘Teach him how to gracefully lose.’ I was used to coming top of my class. But I realised that, even if you win three or four times, the next victory will not necessarily be yours without trying – and also that sometimes it’s better to tell your own story. I started writing my own speeches and changing the way I delivered them, from my heart rather than from a sheet of paper.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">名次并不重要，因为林肯在给儿子老师的信里还写道：“请教导他如何当个有风度的败将。”我已经习惯当班上的第一名了，但我发现，就算你已经连续赢了三四次，如果不够努力，下次的冠军不见得一定还是你。而且有时候，你自己的故事才是最好的故事。于是我开始自己写讲稿，并改变演讲的方式：不再只是读稿子，而是让文字从心里流出来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我能为您做些什么吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我想买几个信封。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 您要哪种信封？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 普通的就行。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 您要买几个？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 买5个。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 给您。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谢谢。顺便问一下，你能告诉我寄张明信片到新加坡要多少钱吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 可以。我查一下……嗯，要花4元5角。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好吧。那给我4元5角钱的邮票吧，我寄这张明信片用。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 给您。如果需要的话，胶水在那边。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谢谢。总共多少钱？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 5元钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好的，给你钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What can I do for you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'd like to buy some envelopes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What kind of envelopes do you need?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Regular ones will do.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How many do you want to buy?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I need five.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Here you are.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thank you. By the way, would you tell me how much it is to send a postcard to Singapore?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Sure. Let me check...well, it will cost you 4.5 yuan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: All right. Then give me 4.5 yuan stamps for this postcard.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Here you are. The glue is over there if you need.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thank you. How much is it in all?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Five.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Okay. Here is the money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That day after our chat, he walked away with both my pen and the lighter.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那天聊完天以后，他就__________把我的钢笔和打火机都拿走了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">顺手牵羊</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section you</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">All I really want to do is be friends with border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. compete beat cheat mistreat 押韵 /i:t/</strong></p><p textvalue="1.     点击链接跳转回顾【ain't】"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 点击链接跳转回顾【ain't】</strong></a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：compete with/against... 与... 竞争</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【“竞争”有关的英语】">点击链接跳转回顾【“竞争”有关的英语】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We can't<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> compete with</strong></em></span> them on price.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在价格上无法<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">与</strong>他们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">竞争</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I had to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">compete </strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">against </strong></em></span>19 other people for the job.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我得和另外19个人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">竞争</strong>这份工作。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...that I was doing it to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">compete against</strong></em></span> Bobby.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说我做这事是为了和鲍比<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">竞争</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;">compete with </strong></em></span>me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果他是想要跟我<strong style="box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. mistreat v. mis- “错误、坏” -treat n. “款待，对待“</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mistreat = 虐待</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：ill-treat ；maltreat</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think people who <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mistreat </strong></em></span>their pets should be banned from keeping them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我认为<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">虐待</strong>宠物的人应当被禁止养宠物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-Sit the fuck down！-You can‘t <span style="color: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-给老子坐下！-你不能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">虐</strong>囚。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. -ify </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">动词后缀</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> “使...；...化” </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">simple + -ify ；simplify v. 使简单，简化</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">class + ify；classify v. 把…归入一类； 将…分类</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cruci- “cross 交叉”+ -fy；crucify v. 把…钉在十字架上处死；严惩；折磨</strong></p><p border-box;">5. defy v. 违抗；反抗；蔑视</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wouldn't have dared to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;">不听</strong>老师的话。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...people who openly <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">defy </strong></em></span>the law</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">公然<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">抗拒</strong>法律的人</p><p style="white-space: 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句</strong></span>：It does <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: It does defy consensus.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它确实<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">违背了</strong>一个简单的答案，它确实违背了共识。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句</strong></span>：I'm gonna <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">defy </strong></span></em>that expectation.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">打破/违背</strong>这个期望。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hollywood...It's a town that's always attracted a certain kind of woman.She arrives, ready to do battle with lipstick and cleavages as her weapons of choice, She is confident of victory, because she knows what life has taught her that beauty is power. But this is not a story about a woman with power. Oh no. This is about another kind of woman. The middle aged housewife, no one ever talks about.The drab sparrow, no one has time for .The plain Jane who is never invited to the party. She has no beauty to draw upon. No style. No grace. This timid creature moves through life as if invisible. Still, she never complains. Years of neglect of have taught her not to expect too much from life. She's been told it's best to wait . That one day the meek shall inherit the earth. Yes, this is the story of Alma Fillcot. A very meek woman, who one day got tired of waiting.</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;max-width: 0px;">单调乏味的；缺乏生气的</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">英释：If you describe something as drab, you think that it is dull and boring to look at or experience.</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句<br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"/>I refuse to ride on a <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">drab </span>float.</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">我才不要坐这么</span><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 77);overflow-wrap: break-word;"><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">例句</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's indeed a <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">plain Jane.</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她真的长着一张<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">大众脸</span>。</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">With her <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">plain Jane</span>, middle-aged looks and her no-nonsense approach to life, Susan is perhaps the most unlikely star to be discovered of late.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在当今社会，以她<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">平凡的外表</span>，中年人的样子和她严肃的生活态度，苏珊或许是最不可能被发掘的明星。</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">良言一句三冬暖，恶语伤人六月寒，还是要多多赞美、欣赏别人哦～</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">1. You are so charming. </p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">charming迷人的，有魅力的；可爱的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He comes across as very concerned, friendly, <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">charming</span>.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他给人的印象很关心他人、很友好、也<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: girl.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">罗丝是个<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">迷人</span>且讨人喜欢的女孩。</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: rgb(47, 138, 77);overflow-wrap: break-word;"><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: You take my breath away. 你美得令人窒息。</span></p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><span style="text-size-adjust: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;">take one's break away让人无法呼吸；使人感到震惊、喜悦或者震撼</span></p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">例句</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wanna find an amazing dress and totally <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To the person who <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">takes my breath away</span>, my beautiful wife, Larsa.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">感谢那个<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">让我为之倾倒</span>的人，我美丽的妻子，拉莎。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">At times, he said the beauty around him <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">took his breath away</span>.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">补充一个单词：breathtaking 形容美得让人窒息，常常说风景，也可用来指人</p><p style="max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">例句</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He watched the <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">breathtaking</span> match to the end.</p><p 87);box-sizing: border-box;">breathtaking</span><span style="text-align: unset;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-size-adjust: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;">. </span><br style="box-sizing: a particular purpose</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句<br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"/><span 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">walk off   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. take without permission  离开</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Alice got up and walked off without saying goodbye. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱丽丝起身，然后连再见都没说就走了出去。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">past  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">prep. up to and beyond a person or place, without stopping经过，越过:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Will you be going past my house on your way home?你回家的路上会经过我家吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">passerby 过路者，行人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hear 和 listen to，后者指听见并加以注意:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You should listen to my advice 你应该听从我的建议。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(NOT You should hear my advice). </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">doll</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. child's toy that looks like a small person or baby玩偶，玩具娃娃:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">living doll 洋娃娃</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nesting doll 俄罗斯套娃 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. Cold-fashioned informal a word meaning an attractive young woman – now usually considered offensive俊妞，美人儿〔现通常被视为具有冒犯性〕:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hey, doll, why don't you get me a cup of coffee? </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">嗨，大美人，干嘛不给我来杯咖啡？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">find it +adj + to do sth的结构中，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">it是做形式宾语，后面的to do不定式才是真正的宾语</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> understand <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that</em> it was just for fun</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">and it will worry Mother</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">她们不会明白那只是为了好玩儿，妈妈会担心的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ONE FINE OCTOBER day when I was still in primary school our desks started to tremble and shake.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Our classes were still mixed at that age, and all the boys and girls yelled, ‘Earthquake!’ We ran outside as we had been taught to do.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All the children gathered around our teachers as chicks swarm to a mother hen.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Swat lies on a geological fault line and we often had earthquakes, but this felt different.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10月一个晴朗的日子，当时我还在读小学，忽然感觉我们的课桌椅开始剧烈地摇晃、晃动起来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为年纪还小，我们都还是男女合班上课。男孩女孩们都开始大叫地震了，边喊边往外跑，就像学校平时教导我们的一样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有的孩子都聚在老师们的身旁，像是小鸡在寻求母鸡的保护。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">斯瓦特坐落在一条地质断层带上，所以这里经常发生地震，但这次的地震不太寻常。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 谁呀？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 先生，客房送餐服务。我把您点的午餐送来了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 谢谢。稍等一下，我在卫生间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 放在电视旁边就行。我没有看到我点的红酒，你是不是忘了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 没有忘，先生。它就在走廊的推车里面。我不想把它摔了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 很好。我喜欢吃饭时配红酒。红酒会让所有的饭菜尝起来味道都浓郁很多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 先生，您想叫我帮您开瓶子吗？或者我可以给您留一个开瓶器您自己开？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 非常感谢。我自己来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 请慢用！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 谢谢！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Who is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Room Service, sir. I have the lunch you ordered.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thanks. Hold on a second. I'm in the bathroom.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Just by the TV. I don't see the bottle of red wine I ordered. Did you forget it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, sir. It's in the hallway waiting on my cart. I didn't want to drop it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Excellent. I love wine with my meal. It makes everything taste so much fuller.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Would you like me to open the bottle. sir? Or I could leave a corkscrew for you to do it yourself?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thanks. I'll take care of it myself.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Enjoy!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thanks!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What’s the sense in borrowing from Zhang just to pay Li？That’s meant to rob Peter to pay Paul.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你从张家借钱还李家有什么意义？那只是__________________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">拆了东墙补西墙</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;">ng 单词内部元元连读；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. ...</strong><strong style="box-sizing: 作指示代词，不弱读。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. overrated  adj. 评价过高的，高估的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In my opinion, she's <span style="text-decoration: underline;">a hugely <span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">overrated </strong></em></span>singer</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">依我所见，她是位被大大<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吹捧过头的</strong>歌手。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I‘ll tell you something. Passion is way <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">overrated</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但是我得告诉你一件事，大家都太<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">高估</strong>激情了<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKeoHvaKercGwcZ8SHMVgP51NDU43Zk6DMFW51c1qIsktFToUicTRDqAXTcw4h6n60lLvg0tWVE0rRg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：expect XX from XX 从某人那里指望某物 </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her parents <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">expected </strong></em></span>high standards from her</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的父母对她的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">期望</strong>很高。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">expect </strong></em></span>good results from our employees.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">期待</strong>员工绩效良好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. ① screw up 犯大错；做蠢事 = mess up</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She realized that she had <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screwed up</strong></em></span> her life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她意识到她把自己的生活都给<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">毁了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You’d better not <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screw up</strong></em></span> this time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这次你最好别<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搞砸了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653521206&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=bfa11c16f93bc1e070f9f01274e0d045&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【“事情搞砸啦！”用英语怎么说？】">点击链接跳转回顾【“事情搞砸啦！”用英语怎么说？】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② screwed-up（screwed-up） adj. 焦虑不安的，神经质的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an extremely <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screwed-up </strong></em></span>kid</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一个十分<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">神经质的</strong>孩子</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's <span style="text-decoration: underline;">been really <span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screwed up</strong></em></span> ever since</span> he lost his job.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自从失业以来，他真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一团糟</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</span></strong>：That's really <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screwed up</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一团糟</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：Don't be afraid to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screw up</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不要害怕（把事情）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搞砸</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm sorry I <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screw up</strong></em></span> all the time! No, Gene you didn't <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">screw up</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对不起我总是把事情<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搞砸</strong>，不吉恩，你没<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搞砸</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: border-box;">很早以前我就发觉很多同学遇到一些问题无处求解。后来，我从2016年起在微博设立“Gwen为你答”板块，免费为大家答疑。几年来，遇到了不少共性的好问题。最近忽然想到，不如把微博上的答疑“搬”来公号，做个集合，供有同样疑问的宝子们查阅参考。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">想法不如行动，说干就干。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将近一年的答疑按照不同类别分成了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活、学习</strong>（语音 口语 听力 原版书 写作）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和推荐</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">类</strong>。暂定每周三更新。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">答疑一直在继续。如果你有什么问题，可随时来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">微博TeacherGwen</strong>私信我。只要我能帮得上忙，都会尽力解答。</span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">口语怎么学？如何输入和输出？</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">在其他人还在私信问我这些问题的时候，有位同学通读了我的方法论文章（<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">听写好难，怎么办？</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">很多宝子反映听写好难，听不懂。那么我们来聊聊“好难”。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">“难”要分两个维度：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 你认为难，别人也认为难吗？我听了一遍感觉并不难，词都抓到了，空也都能填上。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">2. 你现在认为难，三个月后还会认为难吗？如果你现在因难而放弃了，那么它会一直“难”下去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你要解决的是“为什么我认为难”的问题。是因为素材里的单词不认识？语速不适合？还是发音技巧不了解？<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">找出问题对症下药就好了。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">光是抱怨“难”，不是解决问题的态度。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">如何学好一门外语？</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1. 学外语的主要目的是了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">解对方说话内容</strong>，以及<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">能清楚表达自己意思</strong>（至于犯错，无所谓）</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大量听听听，校对后继续听听听</strong>；</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">3. 背单词的方法：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">尽量多涉猎各种素材</strong>，让同一个单词在不同语境中反复出现以加深记忆，而不是背单词表；</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4. 学习一门语言，了解那个国家的文化。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将近一年的答疑按照不同类别分成了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活、学习</strong>（语音 口语 听力 原版书 写作）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和推荐</strong><strong border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">听写好难，怎么办？</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">很多宝子反映听写好难，听不懂。那么我们来聊聊“好难”。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">“难”要分两个维度：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 你认为难，别人也认为难吗？我听了一遍感觉并不难，词都抓到了，空也都能填上。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">2. 你现在认为难，三个月后还会认为难吗？如果你现在因难而放弃了，那么它会一直“难”下去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你要解决的是“为什么我认为难”的问题。是因为素材里的单词不认识？语速不适合？还是发音技巧不了解？<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">找出问题对症下药就好了。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">光是抱怨“难”，不是解决问题的态度。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">如何学好一门外语？</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1. 学外语的主要目的是了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">解对方说话内容</strong>，以及<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">能清楚表达自己意思</strong>（至于犯错，无所谓）</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大量听听听，校对后继续听听听</strong>；</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">3. 背单词的方法：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">尽量多涉猎各种素材</strong>，让同一个单词在不同语境中反复出现以加深记忆，而不是背单词表；</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4. 学习一门语言，了解那个国家的文化。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin:
