border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Supper</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(n.) UK/'sʌpə/ US/'sʌpɚ/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①Some people refer to the main meal eaten in the early part of the evening as supper. 晚餐</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g." Supper, " said the boy. " We're going to have supper."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“晚饭，”孩子说。“我们就来吃吧。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②Supper is a simple meal eaten just before you go to bed at night. 夜宵</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Last Supper, a painting (1495-1497) by Italian artist Leonardo da Vinci.最后的晚餐</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Manage</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(v.)UK/'mænɪdʒ/ US/'mænɪdʒ/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">V-I If you manage, you succeed in coping with a difficult situation. 成功应对</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.I can do it/handle it/deal with it/manage it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我能行、我能做到。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Enjoy oneself =have a good time玩得开心、玩得愉快</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fortnight</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(n.) UK/'fɔːtnaɪt/ US/'fɔrtnaɪt/two weeks: a period of 14 days两个星期；十四天</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.I wish to be crowned within the fortnight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“我希望在两周内完成加冕。--《冰与火之歌》</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dress </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/dres/ US/drɛs/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dress up(vi.) dress formally: to put on formal or especially elegant clothes, usually for a special occasion such as a party盛装打扮</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.I told him he had to dress up tonight,and he got all uptight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我让他今晚穿好点，他就变得紧张起来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Afterwards </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(adv.)UK/'æftɚwɚdz/ US/'æftɚwɚdz/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">after that: at a later time or after an event that has been mentioned previously后来，过后，然后</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.The difference is you didn't disappear afterwards.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">区别在于 之后你有没有消失。---《瑞克与莫蒂 第一季》</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;">我今晚不是麦格，她说。我是一个做疯狂事的玩具娃娃。明天我就变好了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 19px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> to as many young men a</span><span white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">She was sick all the next day</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span Saturday went home</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(64, 64, 64);box-sizing: border-box;">由于两个星期的玩乐，她感到很累</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 19px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 80);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 19px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">I'm glad to be home</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">she sai</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> to her mother an</span><span style="text-decoration: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> Jo</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">after telling them how she was dress</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">p like a doll</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">dran</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">k</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> too much wine</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">and was ill afterwards</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 19px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">真高兴回家来，当她向母亲和琼讲述了她怎样被打扮得像个玩具娃娃、怎样喝了太多的葡萄酒、后来感到难受的事后，她说。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think when there is a great disaster or our lives are in danger we remember our sins and wonder how we will meet God and whether we will be forgiven.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But God has also given us the power to forget, so that when the tragedy is over we carry on as normal. I trusted in my father’s faith, but I also shared my mother’s very real concerns.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我意识到，当巨大的灾难降临，或当我们的生命遭受威胁时，作为信徒的我们就会想起自身曾犯下的罪行，并思索我们何时会遇见真主，而他是否会赦免我们的过错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但同时，真主也赋予了我们遗忘的能力，因此当不幸的事件结束后，我们也能够像一般人一样继续活下去。我不质疑父亲的信念，但也能理解母亲当时非常现实的考虑。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 这是北京烤鸭。这道著名的北京莱从元朝的时候就有了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 看上去不错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 吃起来也很棒。我们餐馆是有着数百年历史的餐馆，因专长做这道菜而闻名。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 能告诉我怎么吃吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 当然可以了。先把鸭肉在甜面酱里蘸一下。然后放在面饼上，再放上一段葱丝，之后把它卷起来。请品尝。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 嗯，确实很好吃。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 请慢用。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: This is the Peking Duck. It's a famous Beijing dish that has been around since the Yuan Dynasty.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It looks good.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It also tastes good. Our centuries-old restaurant is well known for specializing in this particular dish.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Can you tell me how to eat it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Of course. Dip the duck meat into the sweet bean sauce. Then place it onto the pancake, together with a sprig of onion, and wrap it into a roll. Please have a try.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Mmm. It does taste great.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Please enjoy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He had nothing left to desire in life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的生活已经是___________了</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完美无缺</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 包含易错音组/eɪn/；</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. wanting 美音中可发成 /ˈwɑːnt̬ɪŋ/ 或 /ˈwɑːnɪŋ/， border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“jaw”是“下巴”的意思，我们感到“吃惊、惊讶”的时候，下巴难免不自觉的向下“掉”！其实这个表达着实生动形象了！</p><p dropped</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我看见他穿着西装，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">下巴都惊掉</strong>了<span style="font-size: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">日常生活中，除了“jaw drop”之外，我们会比较常见和常用的还有下面这几个表达~</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropping</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">( informal) so large or good that it amazes you </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人大惊失色的；令人咋舌的</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropp</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ing</strong> 6 million dollars </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人吃惊的</strong> 600 万巨款</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The production is absolutely <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropping</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这部作品真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人叫绝</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美艳得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">让人见了合不拢嘴的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那我们在学习英语发音的时候，也会有下巴下沉的时候，也是酱紫来表达啦～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: border-box;">Jaw drops</strong> for the beginning of the diphthong and the back of the tongue lifts.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在读双元音的时候，一开始<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">下巴下沉</strong>，然后舌头抬高<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“jaw”是“下巴”的意思，我们感到“吃惊、惊讶”的时候，下巴难免不自觉的向下“掉”！其实这个表达着实生动形象了！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please don't let your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw drop</strong> when you hear this brilliant news.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">听到这个爆炸新闻之后，千万不要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吃惊</strong>哦！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br dropped</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我看见他穿着西装，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">下巴都惊掉</strong>了<span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">日常生活中，除了“jaw drop”之外，我们会比较常见和常用的还有下面这几个表达~</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropping</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">( informal) so large or good that it amazes you </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人大惊失色的；令人咋舌的</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropp</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ing</strong> 6 million dollars </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人吃惊的</strong> 600 万巨款</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The production is absolutely <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">jaw-dropping</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这部作品真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人叫绝</strong>。</p><p border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无意间想到</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">randomly thought of you </strong>when I saw that cute rabbit.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看到那个小兔子后，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无意间</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想到了你</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">canned peaches 黄桃罐头</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfE05P7B6GXVswmPfA09sHQJFoGvuicj0icRUvBY44O8zGGANN2UCa2z2l6Kic4KgZpdViazPC9c0MofA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="600" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I really enjoy <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">canned peaches.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我真的太爱<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">黄桃罐头</strong>了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">condensed milk 炼乳</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 4px;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 3.2px 3.2px 8px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfE05P7B6GXVswmPfA09sHQHQmNRJ7mBzHLN9vQyQh8QP9MotiaDE1uibibrPXncQsu4m5u6znPWiaYFw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Condensed milk</strong> is cow's milk from which water has been removed (roughly 60% of it).</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炼乳</strong>是牛奶去除水分后得到的物质(大约60%的水分会被去除)。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">就是任性！</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.5" numbers</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你可爱<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炫耀数字</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 1.6;letter-spacing: 3px;padding: 0px 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(230, 154, 88, 0.26);box-sizing: border-box;"> TeacherGwen </span></p></section></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Smooth   /smuːð/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Verb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to move your hands across something in order to make it flat抚平；（使）平整</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He straightened his tie nervously and smoothed his hair.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他紧张地整了整自己的领带，捋了捋头发。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to remove difficulties and make something easier to do or achieve使顺利，使顺畅</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：We encourage parents to help smooth their children's way through</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">school.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们鼓励父母让自己的孩子通过求学铺平人生之路。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to cover the surface of something with a liquid or soft substance, using gentle rubbing movements搽，抹</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pour some oil into the palm of your hand and then smooth it over your </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">arms and neck.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往手掌中倒一点油，然后轻轻涂在手臂和脖子上。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：having a surface or consisting of a substance that is perfectly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">regular and has no holes, lumps, or areas that rise or fall suddenly光滑的，平滑的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The road ahead was flat and smooth.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">前面的路平坦光滑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：happening without any sudden changes, interruption, or</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">difficulty顺利的，流畅的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We had a very smooth flight with no turbulence at all.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们的飞行很顺利，没有碰到强气流。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：having a pleasant flavour that is not sour or bitter醇和的，醇香的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This coffee is incredibly smooth and rich.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这种咖啡的味道醇香浓郁。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：very polite, confident, and able to persuade people, but in a way that is not sincere圆滑的，能说会道的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The deputy director is so smooth that many of his colleagues distrust</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> him.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个副主任非常圆滑，他的很多同事都不信任他。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Red 流血、危险、暴力、热情</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子： </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">red flag 红旗；危险的信号</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">red ruin 火灾</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">red battle 血战</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">green活力、生长、希望、青春、钱财、嫉妒、眼红</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">green worker 学徒工</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">green-eyed 眼红</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">white  幸福、纯洁</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a white day 吉日</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">white war 不流血的战争</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">white lie 无恶意的谎言</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blue 情绪低落、社会地位高、出身名门、黄色的、下流的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the blues 忧郁</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blue blood 贵族血统</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blue talk 下流的言论</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">yellow 胆小、怯懦、卑鄙</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a yellow dog 卑鄙的人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">yellow streak 胆小鬼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">black坏的、邪恶的、气愤</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">black market 黑市</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">black sheep 害群之马</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">black in the face 脸色铁青</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gossip  /ˈɡɑː.səp/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：conversation or reports about other people's private lives that might be unkind, disapproving, or not true（有关别人隐私的）流言蜚语，闲言碎语，闲聊</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her letter was full of gossip.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她信里讲的都是些闲言碎语。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：someone who enjoys talking about other people and their</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">private lives爱说长道短的人；喜欢散布流言蜚语的人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's a terrible gossip.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她是个很要命的长舌妇。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to talk about other people's private lives（对别人的隐私）说长道短，传播流言蜚语</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Stop gossiping and do your work.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别再闲扯了，继续干点活去。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wicked</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective  /ˈwɪk.ɪd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：morally wrong and bad邪恶的；坏的；缺德的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was a wicked thing to do.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那是件缺德的事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：slightly immoral or bad for you, but in an attractive way顽皮的；恶作剧的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a wicked grin</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">淘气的一笑</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：excellent优秀的；棒的；极好的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That car is wicked!</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那辆车太棒了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘At night our fear is strong, Jani,’ he told me, ‘but in the morning, in the light, we find our courage again.’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And this is true for my family. We were scared, but our fear was not as strong as our courage.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“夜晚，人们的恐惧会增强，亲爱的。” 他告诉我，”但是天亮了之后，大地一片光明之时，我们会再次找到自己的勇气。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对我们的家人来说，的确如此。我们很害怕，但我们的勇气远胜于恐惧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 早上好。需要帮忙吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是的。我想看看你们的山地车系列。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的，我们这儿有一种新型号。就是那边的那辆。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 能给我介绍一下吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的。这款产品适合十岁以上的孩子，有男式车和女式车。男式车有黄色和紫色两种颜色，女式车有灰色和粉红色。这种车上市刚几个月，但相当受欢迎。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 多少钱一辆？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 450元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 样式和颜色是很好看，就是价钱贵了点儿。可以打折吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 抱歉不可以。像这样的新产品通常不打折。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Good morning. Can I help you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. I'm interested in your range of mountain bikes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, we've got a new model here. It's that one over there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Can you tell me something about it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes. It's suitable for children from the age of ten and over. We have a boy's model and a girl's model. The boy's is available in yellow and purple and the girl's is available in grey and pink. It's been on the market for just a few months, but it's quite popular.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: How much does it cost?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It costs 450 yuan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The design and color are very beautiful. but it's a little expensive. Is there any discount?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Sorry. Not usually on new products like this.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Your criticism of him fitted just like a glove. If you had made it a bit hotter, he could not have possibly accepted them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你对他的批评___________，如果你说得再过点儿头，他也许就接受不了了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恰到好处</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: You don't just become best friends.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. mu‧tu‧al /ˈmjuːtʃuəl/ 三音节单词，单词内部元元连读会带出 /w/；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. friendship中的/d/ 不完全爆破。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. Friendship takes time and years of mutual care and respect.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">友谊需要时间，以及长久的互相关心和尊重。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">take v. 花费/需要〔时间、金钱或努力等〕</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">took </strong></em></span>me ages to find a present for Dad.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">花了</strong>很长时间才买到一样给爸爸的礼物</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">takes </strong></em></span>courage to admit you are wrong.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">承认错误<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">需要</strong>勇气。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：mutual care and respect 互相关心和尊重</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual adj. 相互的，彼此的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual respect/trust/understanding 相互尊重/信任/理解</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：mutual 本来是“互相”的意思。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual aid 互助，但是意义扩大到“共同”</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;box-sizing: border-box;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mutual fund 共同基金（美国的一种投资方式）</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mutual friend 共同的朋友</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mutual hobby 共同的爱好</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mutual effort 共同努力</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We have a <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual </strong></em></span>interest in opera.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">咱们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">都对</strong>歌剧<span style="color: rgb(22, 21, 21);box-sizing: border-box;">感</span>兴趣。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：... and work together towards that <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual </strong></em></span>goal.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">... 为<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">共同的</strong>目标共同努力。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：We can have some <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual </strong></em></span>respect for each other.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">互相</strong>尊重。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...as a symbolic way of showing our <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mutual </strong></em></span>independence?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作为我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">彼此</strong>独立的标志可以吗？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" I'm the girl who shows up, not the girl who makes bad decisions. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: You're not the only one making decisions here.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Well, I'm the only one who's getting fired tomorrow.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Maybe losing your job wouldn't be so bad. Take a year to travel. Eat good food.Fall in love.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Gonna have to let me eat for free at your restaurant.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: I'm not gonna have a restaurant.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: What about the loan from Camille's family?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: If I take money from them, they own me.I don't wanna be owned by anyone. Even if it means<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> putting my dreams on hold for a while</strong>.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: It's better 0px 21px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频之后，你是否已经找到了今天的主题表达了呢？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：If I take money from them, they own me.I don't wanna be owned by anyone. Even if it means<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> putting my dreams on hold </strong>for a while.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put XX on hold 搁置XX；让XX等待; 暂停XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：Some summer vacation plans have been <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put on hold</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>有些夏季假期计划也<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搁置</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：</strong>I'm gonna have to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put you on hold</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">先等等</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">想表达搁置；暂停; 暂且不理..还有很多其它的表达。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">beat oneself up 自我责备</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 15px 0% 26px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(111, 100, 141);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 21px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: She ran away, and you're here, and you're going to fix it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br 自我责备</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p up </strong>for others' mistakes. 你不需要为了别人的错误<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自我责备</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: I'm the girl who shows up, not the girl who makes bad decisions. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: You're not the only one making decisions here.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Well, I'm the only one who's getting fired tomorrow.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Maybe losing your job wouldn't be so bad. Take a year to travel. Eat good food.Fall in love.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Gonna have to let me eat for free at your restaurant.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: I'm not gonna have a restaurant.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: What about the loan from Camille's family?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: If I take money from them, they own me.I don't wanna be owned by anyone. Even if it means<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> putting my dreams on hold for a while</strong>.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: It's better 0px 21px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频之后，你是否已经找到了今天的主题表达了呢？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：If I take money from them, they own me.I don't wanna be owned by anyone. Even if it means<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> putting my dreams on hold </strong>for a while.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put XX on hold 搁置XX；让XX等待; 暂停XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：Some summer vacation plans have been <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put on hold</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>有些夏季假期计划也<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">搁置</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：</strong>I'm gonna have to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put you on hold</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">先等等</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">想表达搁置；暂停; 暂且不理..还有很多其它的表达。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;border-left: 1px dashed rgb(0, 0, 0);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;border-right: 1px dashed rgb(0, 0, 0);border-top-right-radius: 0px;padding: 5px 8px;flex: 8 8 0%;height: auto;align-self: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -15px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;border-top: 1px dashed rgb(111, 100, 141);border-top-left-radius: 0px;padding: 10px 0px;border-bottom: 1px dashed rgb(111, 100, 141);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: style="box-sizing: border-box;">01</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;letter-spacing: 2px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;color: rgb(111, 100, 141);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put XX aside 暂且放在一边</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 15px 0% 26px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(111, 100, 141);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 21px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：let us <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put all the mystery aside</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>让我们把这些谜团<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">暂且搁置一边</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;border-left: 1px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick XX into the long grass 搁置；置之不理</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(111, 100, 141);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：It looks like you're going to have to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick that drink into the long grass</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>看来这杯你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">暂时喝不到</strong>了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">beat oneself up 自我责备</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 15px 0% 26px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(111, 100, 141);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 21px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">beating yourself up</strong>. She ran away, and you're here, and you're going to fix it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链：beat oneself up 自我责备</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p up </strong>for others' mistakes. 你不需要为了别人的错误<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自我责备</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">together</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">你们会的，你们会的。麦格和琼异口同声地说道。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My father used to say the people of Swat and the teachers would continue to educate our children until the last room, the last teacher and the last student was alive.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My parents never once suggested I should withdraw from school, ever. Going to school, reading and doing our homework wasn’t just a way of passing time, it was our future.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">父亲以前总说，只要还有一间教室、一名老师和一个学生存在，斯瓦特的人们和老师们就不会放弃他们对孩子的教育。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我的父母从未想过让我放弃学业。到学校上课、阅读和写作业并不仅仅是为了度过光阴，我们的未来与之息息相关。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 请把账单给我，好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好的，先生，我立刻就给您拿来。给您。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 多少钱？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 总共150元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 嗯，我觉得不对。听起来对于我点的东西来说有点太贵了。请再检查一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对不起，先生。让我再看看账单。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我认为你们多收了我10块钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 啊，是的，先生。您说得对。对此我向您道歉。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 没关系。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我希望今天的饭菜都做得不错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 是的，非常不错。以前我从没来过这里，但是我的朋友们都建议我来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 很高兴您的朋友们也喜欢这里的饭菜。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Could I have my bill, please?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, sir. I'll be back right away. Here you are.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How much is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: One hundred and fifty altogether.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, I think there's a mistake. Sounds a little too expensive for what was ordered. Please check it again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm sorry, sir. Let me look at the bill again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I think you've overcharged me ten yuan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Ah, yes, sir. You are right. I do apologize for it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It doesn't matter.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I hope everything was excellent today.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes. it was great. I've never been here before. but my friends recommended I come.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm glad your friends liked it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why should you always sing that guy’s praises? I don’t think he deserves all your praise.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你为什么老是_______那个家伙？我认为他不值得你称赞。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">赞扬</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: What they don't realize is you're just as screwed up as they are.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">与 screw up 含义相近的词组为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A make up   B mess up   C bulk up</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552571&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=be8d29797f5fd20eb2f026b850cf177d&amp;chksm=f7e83f76c09fb660443c0e833037fbe253bb71bda4cd356c0ccf138509e764810d6db866c599&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="4.We do strange things for the people we love. There may be some bumps along the way. But we never stop wanting the best for them.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">strange正确的音标是？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A /strendʒ/    B /strəndʒ/    C  /streɪndʒ/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552605&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=9b2d79dc0e249df4822caa4b03fd6560&amp;chksm=f7e83f10c09fb6065091be492e29cce2c34faf4146eb0f64fa4f817ed9f8237897027dfbeb59&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. Friendship takes time and years of mutual care and respect. You don't just become best friends.">5. Friendship takes time and years of mutual care and respect. You don't just become best friends.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">friendship 单词内部 /d/ 的发音在语音学上被称为？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 不完全爆破   B 失去爆破   C 省音</p></section></section><section style="height: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width: 24px;float:
